<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">REPORT OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM</font></u></b><a name="ReportOfIndependentRegisteredPubl_061741"></a></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To Participants and Administrative Committee of</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have audited the accompanying statement of net assets available for benefits of The Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan as of December&nbsp;31, 2011 and 2010, and the related statements of changes in net assets available for benefits for the years then ended.&#160; These financial statements are the responsibility of the Plan&#146;s management.&#160; Our responsibility is to express an opinion on these financial statements based on our audits.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We conducted our audits in accordance with standards of the Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (United States).&#160; Those standards require that we plan and perform the audit to obtain reasonable assurance about whether the financial statements are free of material misstatement.&#160; An audit includes examining, on a test basis, evidence supporting the amounts and disclosures in the financial statements.&#160; An audit also includes assessing the accounting principles used and significant estimates made by management, as well as evaluating the overall financial statement presentation.&#160; We believe that our audits provide a reasonable basis for our opinion.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In our opinion, the financial statements referred to above present fairly, in all material respects, the net assets available for benefits of the Plan as of December&nbsp;31, 2011 and 2010, and the changes in its net assets available for benefits for the years then ended in conformity with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our audits were conducted for the purpose of forming an opinion on the basic financial statements taken as a whole.&#160; The accompanying supplemental Schedule of Assets (Held at End of Year) is presented for the purpose of additional analysis and is not a required part of the basic financial statements but is supplementary information required by the Department of Labor&#146;s Rules&nbsp;and Regulations for Reporting and Disclosure under the Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974.&#160; The supplemental schedule is the responsibility of the Plan&#146;s management.&#160; The information has been subjected to the auditing procedures applied in the audits of the financial statements and, in our opinion, is fairly stated in all material respects in relation to the basic financial statements taken as a whole.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THE KROGER CO. 401(K)&nbsp;RETIREMENT SAVINGS ACCOUNT PLAN</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Financial Statements<a name="NotesToFinancialStatements_054924"></a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(All dollar amounts are in thousands)</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.75pt;text-indent:-18.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Description of Plan</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.75pt;text-indent:-18.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following description of The Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan (Plan) provides only general information.&#160; Participants should refer to the plan document for a more complete description of Plan provisions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">General</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan, which began January&nbsp;1, 2007, is sponsored by The Kroger Co., an Ohio corporation, and its wholly-owned subsidiaries (collectively the Company).&#160; The Plan is a defined contribution plan covering all employees of the Company who have attained age 21, have been employed 30 days, and have completed 72 hours of service within the 30-day period, excluding those employees eligible to participate under another defined contribution pension plan or defined benefit pension plan sponsored by the Company.&#160; It is subject to the provisions of the Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974, as amended (ERISA).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Contributions</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participant</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subject to certain limits, participants may contribute up to 75% of compensation per pay period to the Plan.&#160; It is at the discretion of participants to modify and direct investments.&#160; Participants are eligible to make catch-up contributions beginning in the year in which they reach age 50.&#160; Participants are also permitted to deposit into the Plan distributions from other qualified plans.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Employer</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The employer will credit the participant&#146;s account with a match and/or an automatic contribution if the participant meets the eligibility requirements.&#160; The matching contribution is 100% of the first 3% of the participant&#146;s plan compensation contributed as a salary redirection contribution, plus 50% of the next 2% of the participant&#146;s plan compensation contributed as a salary redirection contribution.&#160; At the end of each plan year, the employer will, if necessary, make a &#147;true-up&#148; matching contribution in the first quarter of the following year.&#160; Subject to certain limits, the Company also pays an automatic contribution of 1% or 2% based on the participant&#146;s years of vesting service.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participant Accounts</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each participant account is credited with the participant contribution, matching contribution (if any), automatic contribution, and an allocation of Plan earnings or losses.&#160; Allocations of earnings or losses are based upon the performance of the</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_051740_7056"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\106757\12-15450-1\task5413878\15450-1-bc.htm',USER='106757',CD='Jun 27 13:32 2012' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">investment funds chosen by the participant.&#160; The benefit to which a participant is entitled is the benefit that can be provided from the participant&#146;s vested account.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Vesting</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With the exception of amounts transferred from The Little Clinic LLC 401(k)&nbsp;Plan, all employee contributions, employer matching contributions, transferred accounts, and rollover accounts are fully vested at all times.&#160; The participant&#146;s vested interest in all automatic contributions, if any, will be determined based upon the participant&#146;s years of vesting service with the employer.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In regards to transfers from The Little Clinic LLC 401(k)&nbsp;Plan to this Plan, effective January&nbsp;1, 2011, the vested percentage of the portion of the participant&#146;s matching account from The Little Clinic LLC 401(k)&nbsp;Plan shall be determined by years of service.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Benefits</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payment of benefits can be made under various methods, depending upon the reason for the distribution, such as termination of service, death, or retirement, as well as other factors.&#160; At termination, those participants with a balance of less than or equal to one thousand dollars will receive a single lump sum distribution.&#160; Absent specific elections by the participant, those with balances greater than one thousand dollars and less than or equal to five thousand dollars shall be distributed, in the form of a direct rollover, to an individual retirement account designated by the Plan Administrator.&#160; Those with balances greater than five thousand dollars may elect to leave their funds in the Plan or choose other options.&#160; Participants are entitled to benefits beginning at normal retirement age (generally age 65).&#160; Benefits are recorded when paid.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes Receivable from Participants</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan permits participants to borrow from their vested account less all vested automatic contributions and matching contributions.&#160; The maximum amount that may be borrowed is the lesser of fifty thousand dollars or 50% of the vested balance of the account.&#160; Loan terms range from 1 - 4 years or up to 6 years for the purchase of a primary residence.&#160; The loans are collateralized by the balance in the participant&#146;s account and bear interest at a rate of Prime plus 1.0%.&#160; The rate is changed quarterly and the Prime rate used for a quarter is the Prime rate on the last business day of the previous quarter.&#160; Principal and interest are paid through periodic payroll deductions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes receivable from participants are measured at their unpaid principal balance plus any accrued but unpaid interest. Delinquent notes receivable from participants are recorded as a distribution based on the terms of the Plan document.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_051800_5335"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Forfeitures</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Forfeited balances shall be applied in the following order: to restore the accounts of any participants who return to service of the employer and again become eligible employees prior to incurring a five year period of severance, to reduce administrative services of the Plan, and to reduce any Company Automatic Contributions for the Plan year. The balance of forfeitures was $397 and $185 at December&nbsp;31, 2011 and 2010, respectively. For 2011, $397 is being held to be used to reduce administrative services of the Plan.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Summary of Significant Accounting Policies</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Basis of accounting</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The financial statements of the Plan are prepared using the accrual basis of accounting in conformity with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Master Trust</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The investments of the Plan, along with investments of other plans of The Kroger Co. and its subsidiaries, are pooled for investment purposes in a master trust pursuant to an agreement dated July&nbsp;1, 2004, between Bank of America, N.A., as successor in interest to Merrill Lynch Bank&nbsp;&amp; Trust Co., FSB, the trustee, and the Company &#151; The Kroger Defined Contribution Plan Master Trust (the Master Trust).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investment valuation and income recognition</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan&#146;s investments within the Master Trust are stated at fair value.&#160; Fair value is the price that would be received to sell an asset or paid to transfer a liability in an orderly transaction between market participants at the measurement date.&#160; See Note 6 for discussion of fair value measurements.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Purchases and sales of securities are recorded on a trade date basis.&#160; Gains or losses on sales of securities are based on average cost.&#160; Dividends are recorded on the ex-dividend date.&#160; Income from other investments is recorded as earned.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investment contracts held by a defined-contribution plan are required to be reported at fair value.&#160; However, contract value is the relevant measurement attribute for that portion of the net assets available for benefits of a defined-contribution plan attributable to fully benefit-responsive investment contracts because contract value is the amount participants would receive if they were to initiate a permitted transaction under the terms of the Plan. &#160;The Plan invests in investment contracts through the Master Trust.&#160; The Statement of Net Assets Available for Benefits presents the fair value of the investment in the Master Trust as well as the adjustment of the investment in the Master Trust from fair value to contract value relating to investment contracts.&#160; The Statement of Changes in Net Assets Available for Benefits is prepared on a contract value basis.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6<a name="PB_6_051825_5796"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Estimates</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The presentation of financial statements in conformity with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States requires management to make estimates and assumptions that affect certain reported amounts and disclosures.&#160; Actual results may differ from those estimates.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Administrative expenses</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan will pay the administrative costs and expenses of the Plan, including the trustee and management fees.&#160; Any expenses that are unable to be allocated to participants are paid by the Company.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent events</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company evaluates events and transactions occurring subsequent to the date of the financial statements for matters requiring recognition or disclosure in the financial statements. The accompanying financial statements consider events through the date on which the financial statements were available to be issued.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investments</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan provides for participant directed investments into common shares of The Kroger Co., mutual funds, collective trusts, stable value funds, and certain retirement date funds, through the investment in the Master Trust.&#160; Investments that represent 5% or more of the Plan&#146;s net assets as of December&nbsp;31, 2011 and 2010 are as follows:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Included in investment income (loss) from the Plan&#146;s participation in the Master Trust is depreciation of $(25,024) and appreciation of $178,993 at December&nbsp;31, 2011 and 2010, respectively.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Investment Contracts</u>:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Master Trust holds several synthetic investment contracts which are managed by investment fund managers.&#160; The Master Trust also purchases wrapper contracts from financial institutions which provide assurance that crediting rates will never be less than zero.&#160; All Plans have an undivided interest in each investment contract.&#160; The investment contracts are fully benefit responsive.&#160; A fully benefit-responsive investment provides a liquidity guarantee by a financially responsible third party of principal and previously accrued interest for liquidations, transfers, loans, or withdrawals initiated by Plan participants under the terms of the ongoing Plan.&#160; Certain employer-initiated events (i.e. layoffs, mergers, bankruptcy, Plan termination) are not eligible for the liquidity guarantee.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7<a name="PB_7_052040_2897"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>

<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In general, issuers may terminate the investment contracts and settle at other than contract value if the qualification status of the employer or plan changes, breach of material obligations under the contract and misrepresentation by the contract holder, or failure of the underlying portfolio to conform to the pre-established investment guidelines.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan Administrator does not believe that the occurrence of any such event, which would limit the Plan&#146;s ability to transact at contract value with participants, is probable.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="12%" colspan="2" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:12.44%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">29,168</font></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.58%;">

<td width="12%" colspan="2" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:12.44%;">

<td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.58%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:262.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The underlying investments within the synthetic contracts include corporate, government and mortgage backed debt securities.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of December&nbsp;31, 2011 and 2010, the Plan&#146;s interest in the net assets of the Master Trust was 41.51% and 38.95%, respectively.&#160; The Master Trust allocates individual assets to each plan participating in the Master Trust arrangement.&#160; Therefore, the investment results of the Plan may not reflect its proportionate interest in the Master Trust.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9<a name="PB_9_053115_7748"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fair Value Measurements</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For financial statement elements currently required to be measured at fair value, Financial Accounting Standards Board (FASB) defines fair value, establishes a framework for measuring fair value, and expands disclosures about fair value measurements. The standards define fair value as the price that would be received to sell an asset or paid to transfer a liability (exit price) regardless of whether an observable liquid market price exists.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FASB establishes a fair value hierarchy that categorizes the inputs to valuation techniques that are used to measure fair value into three levels:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Level   1 includes observable inputs which reflect quoted prices for identical assets   or liabilities in active markets at the measurement date.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Level   2 includes observable inputs for assets or liabilities other than quoted   prices included in Level 1 and it includes valuation techniques which use   prices for similar assets and liabilities. </font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Level   3 includes unobservable inputs which reflect the reporting entity&#146;s estimates   of the assumptions that market participants would use in pricing the asset or   liability, including assumptions about risk.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The asset&#146;s fair value measurement level within the fair value hierarchy is based on the lowest level of any input that is significant to the fair value measurement. Valuation techniques used need to maximize the use of observable inputs and minimize the use of unobservable inputs.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following is a description of the valuation methods used for assets measured at fair value. There have been no changes in methodologies used at December&nbsp;31, 2011 and 2010.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cash and cash equivalents: </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The carrying   value approximates fair value.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Common Stocks: </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The fair values of these   securities are based on observable market quotations for identical assets and   are valued at the closing price reported on the active market on which the   individual securities are traded.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mutual Funds:</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> The fair values of these   securities are primarily based on observable market quotations for identical   assets and are valued at the closing price reported on the active market on   which the individual securities are traded.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Guaranteed Investment Contracts: The investments   include cash and cash equivalents, fixed maturity guaranteed investment   contracts (GICs) and constant duration GICs. The fair value of the   investments are calculated using the present value of the contract&#146;s future   cash flow values discounted by comparable duration Wall Street Journal GIC   Index rates. Fair values for variable synthetic GICs are calculated using the   present value of the contract&#146;s future cash flow values discounted by   comparable swap rates. Fair values for constant duration synthetic GICs are   calculated using the market values provided by the external investment   managers.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10<a name="PB_10_053857_7608"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Collective Trusts: The collective trust funds are   public investment vehicles valued using a Net Asset Value (NAV) provided by   the manager of each fund.&nbsp; The NAV is   based on the underlying net assets owned by the fund, divided by the number   of shares outstanding.&nbsp; The NAV&#146;s unit   price is quoted on a private market that is not active.&nbsp; However, t</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">he NAV is based on the   fair value of the underlying securities within the fund, which are traded on   an active market, and valued at the closing price reported on the active   market on which those individual securities are traded. The significant   investment strategies of the funds are as described in the financial   statements provided by each fund. There are no restrictions on redemptions   from these funds.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="94%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:27.9pt;width:94.84%;">
<tr>
<td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.52%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="96%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:96.48%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Retirement Date Funds:</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> Retirement date funds are   made up of investments in mutual funds, custom funds, and collective trusts,   and are valued in a manner consistent with that described above.</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The methods described above may produce a fair value calculation that may not be indicative of net realizable value or reflective of future fair values. Furthermore, while the Plan believes its valuation methods are appropriate and consistent with other market participants, the use of different methodologies or assumptions to determine the fair value of certain financial instruments could result in a different fair value measurement.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While all the investments of the participating plans are deemed part of the Master Trust, each plan does maintain a separate accounting of its share of the investments in the Master Trust.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The GICs shown above include wrap contracts, the fair value of which is immaterial</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Income Tax Status</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan has applied for a determination letter in January 2011 but has not yet received a response.&#160; The plan administrator believes that the Plan currently is designed and is currently being operated in compliance with the applicable requirements of the Internal Revenue Code (IRC). Therefore, no provision of income taxes has been included in the Plan&#146;s financial statements.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America require plan management to evaluate tax positions taken by the plan and recognize a tax liability (or asset) if the plan has taken an uncertain position that more likely than not would not be sustained upon examination by the Internal Revenue Service. The plan administrator has analyzed the tax positions taken by the plan, and has concluded that as of December 31, 2011, there are no uncertain positions taken or expected to be taken that would require recognition of a liability (or asset) or disclosure in the financial statements. The plan is subject to routine audits by taxing jurisdictions; however, there are currently no audits for any tax periods in progress. </font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The plan administrator believes it is no longer subject to income tax examinations for the years prior to 2008.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13<a name="PB_13_051514_8146"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Risks and Uncertainties</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan invests in various investment securities.&#160; Investment securities are exposed to various risks such as interest rate, market, and credit risks.&#160; Due to the level of risk associated with certain investment securities, it is at least reasonably possible that changes in the values of investment securities will occur in the near term and that such changes could materially affect participants&#146; account balances and the amounts reported in the statement of net assets available for benefits.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Plan Termination</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Although it has not expressed any intent to do so, the Company has the right under the Plan to terminate the Plan at any time subject to the provisions of ERISA.&#160; In the event of any total or partial termination or discontinuance, the accounts of all affected participants shall remain fully vested and non-forfeitable.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Related-party and Party-in-interest Transactions</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan&#146;s portion of its interest in the Master Trust included $136,319 and $125,523 of The Kroger Co. common shares at December 31, 2011 and 2010, respectively, at fair value.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan purchased 2,924,572 and 2,530,238 common shares of The Kroger Co. at a cost of $67,742 and $54,284 in 2011 and 2010, respectively, through its interest in the Master Trust.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan sold 2,858,121 and 2,310,630 common shares of The Kroger Co. for $66,959 and $50,294 with a realized gain of $2,593 and $944 in 2011 and 2010, respectively, through its interest in the Master Trust.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Bank of America, N.A. and Merrill Lynch provide recordkeeping and investment management services to the Plan.&#160; Therefore, transactions with Bank of America, N.A. and Merrill Lynch qualify as party-in-interest transactions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reconciliation of Financial Statements to Form 5500</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following is a reconciliation of net assets available for plan benefits per the financial statements to the Form 5500:</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Plan Amendment</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Effective January 1, 2011, the Plan was amended to allow current employees of The Little Clinic LLC to participate in the Plan and to authorize and accommodate the merger of The Little Clinic LLC 401(k) Plan in the Plan.&#160; As a result, during 2011, approximately $2,143 was transferred into the Plan.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">15<a name="PB_15_052733_455"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CONSENT OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the Plan Administrator of</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We consent to incorporation by reference in the Registration Statements (No.&nbsp;333-138152 and No.&nbsp;333-180404) on Form&nbsp;S-8 of The Kroger Co. of our report dated June&nbsp;27, 2012, relating to the statements of net assets available for benefits of The Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan as of December&nbsp;31, 2011 and 2010, and the related statements of changes in net assets available for benefits and the supplemental schedules for the years then ended, which report appears in the December&nbsp;31, 2011 annual report on Form&nbsp;11-K of The Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan.</font></p>
